login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.users = {}  # This should be replaced with a secure database
    def login(self, username, password):
        # Simple authentication logic
        return self.users.get(username) == password
    def register(self, username, password):
        # Register a new user
        if username in self.users:
            return False
        self.users[username] = password
        return True
```

logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json
class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()
    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []
    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)
    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False
    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True
    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```

photo_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles photo uploads for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import os
from PIL import Image
class PhotoManager:
    def __init__(self, upload_directory="uploads"):
        self.upload_directory = upload_directory
        if not os.path.exists(self.upload_directory):
            os.makedirs(self.upload_directory)
    def upload_photo(self, photo_path):
        '''
        Uploads a photo to the designated upload directory.
        '''
        try:
            # Open the image to ensure it's valid
            with Image.open(photo_path) as img:
                img.verify()  # Verify that this is an image file
            # Copy the file to the upload directory
            file_name = os.path.basename(photo_path)
            destination_path = os.path.join(self.upload_directory, file_name)
            with open(photo_path, 'rb') as src_file:
                with open(destination_path, 'wb') as dest_file:
                    dest_file.write(src_file.read())
            return destination_path
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to upload photo: {e}")
            return None
```

ocr_manager.py
```python
'''
Integrates OCR functionality for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import pytesseract
from PIL import Image
class OCRManager:
    def process_image(self, image_path):
        # Extract text from image using OCR
        image = Image.open(image_path)
        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image)
        return text
```

cloud_storage_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages cloud storage for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import boto3
class CloudStorageManager:
    def __init__(self, bucket_name):
        self.s3 = boto3.client('s3')
        self.bucket_name = bucket_name
    def upload_file(self, file_path, key):
        self.s3.upload_file(file_path, self.bucket_name, key)
    def download_file(self, key, file_path):
        self.s3.download_file(self.bucket_name, key, file_path)
```

digital_signature_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles digital signatures for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA
class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature
    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```

The highest priority issue in the provided code is the lack of a secure and persistent user authentication system. The current implementation uses a simple dictionary to store user credentials, which is not secure or persistent. This does not meet the requirement for secure login functionality.

**Suggestion for Revision:**
1. Implement a secure and persistent user authentication system using a database (e.g., SQLite, PostgreSQL) to store user credentials securely.
2. Use password hashing (e.g., bcrypt) to store passwords securely instead of storing them in plain text.
3. Consider using a library like Flask-Login for managing user sessions and authentication securely.

Here's a basic example of how you might start implementing these changes using SQLite and bcrypt:

```python
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash

class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()

    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')

    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False

    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

This code uses SQLite for persistent storage and `werkzeug.security` for password hashing, which enhances security and meets the requirement for secure login functionality.

**Suggestion for Revision:**

```python
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash

class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()

    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')

    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False

    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

This code uses SQLite for persistent storage and `werkzeug.security` for password hashing, which enhances security and meets the requirement for secure login functionality.

```python
from kivy.app import App
from kivy.uix.button import Button
from kivy.uix.boxlayout import BoxLayout
from login_manager import LoginManager
from logbook_manager import LogbookManager
from photo_manager import PhotoManager

class MainApp(App):
    def build(self):
        self.login_manager = LoginManager()
        self.logbook_manager = LogbookManager()
        self.photo_manager = PhotoManager()
        self.ocr_manager = OCRManager()
        self.cloud_storage_manager = CloudStorageManager(bucket_name="your_bucket_name")
        self.digital_signature_manager = DigitalSignatureManager(private_key_path="path/to/private_key.pem", public_key_path="path/to/public_key.pem")
        layout = BoxLayout(orientation='vertical')
        login_button = Button(text="Login")
        login_button.bind(on_press=self.login)
        layout.add_widget(login_button)
        return layout
    def login(self, instance):
        # Example login function

        password = "pass"
        if self.login_manager.login(username, password):
            print("Login successful")
        else:
            print("Login failed")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    MainApp().run()
```

login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.users = {}  # This should be replaced with a secure database
    def login(self, username, password):
        # Simple authentication logic
        return self.users.get(username) == password
    def register(self, username, password):
        # Register a new user
        if username in self.users:
            return False
        self.users[username] = password
        return True
```

logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json
class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()
    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []
    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)
    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False
    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True
    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```

photo_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles photo uploads for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import os
from PIL import Image
class PhotoManager:
    def __init__(self, upload_directory="uploads"):
        self.upload_directory = upload_directory
        if not os.path.exists(self.upload_directory):
            os.makedirs(self.upload_directory)
    def upload_photo(self, photo_path):
        '''
        Uploads a photo to the designated upload directory.
        '''
        try:
            # Open the image to ensure it's valid
            with Image.open(photo_path) as img:
                img.verify()  # Verify that this is an image file
            # Copy the file to the upload directory
            file_name = os.path.basename(photo_path)
            destination_path = os.path.join(self.upload_directory, file_name)
            with open(photo_path, 'rb') as src_file:
                with open(destination_path, 'wb') as dest_file:
                    dest_file.write(src_file.read())
            return destination_path
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to upload photo: {e}")
            return None
```

```python
        return text
```

```python
    def upload_file(self, file_path, key):
        self.s3.upload_file(file_path, self.bucket_name, key)
```

digital_signature_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles digital signatures for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA
class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature
    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```

"
Comments on Codes:
"The highest priority issue in the provided code is the lack of a secure and persistent user authentication system. The current implementation uses a simple dictionary to store user credentials, which is not secure or persistent. This does not meet the requirement for secure login functionality.

**Suggestion for Revision:**
1. Implement a secure and persistent user authentication system using a database (e.g., SQLite, PostgreSQL) to store user credentials securely.
2. Use password hashing (e.g., bcrypt) to store passwords securely instead of storing them in plain text.
3. Consider using a library like Flask-Login for managing user sessions and authentication securely.

Here's a basic example of how you might start implementing these changes using SQLite and bcrypt:

```python
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash

class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()

    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')

    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False

    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

This code uses SQLite for persistent storage and `werkzeug.security` for password hashing, which enhances security and meets the requirement for secure login functionality."

login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash

class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()

    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')

    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False

    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json

class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()

    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []

    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)

    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False

    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True

    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```

```python
'''
Handles digital signatures for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA

class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())

    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature

    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```

login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash

class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()

    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')

    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False

    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json

class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()

    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []

    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)

    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False

    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True

    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```

```python
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA

class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())

    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature

    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```

```python
'''
Main application file for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from kivy.app import App
from kivy.uix.button import Button
from kivy.uix.boxlayout import BoxLayout
from login_manager import LoginManager
from logbook_manager import LogbookManager
from photo_manager import PhotoManager
from ocr_manager import OCRManager
from cloud_storage_manager import CloudStorageManager
from digital_signature_manager import DigitalSignatureManager
class MainApp(App):
    def build(self):
        self.login_manager = LoginManager()
        self.logbook_manager = LogbookManager()
        self.photo_manager = PhotoManager()
        self.ocr_manager = OCRManager()
        self.cloud_storage_manager = CloudStorageManager(bucket_name="your_bucket_name")
        self.digital_signature_manager = DigitalSignatureManager(private_key_path="path/to/private_key.pem", public_key_path="path/to/public_key.pem")
        layout = BoxLayout(orientation='vertical')
        login_button = Button(text="Login")
        login_button.bind(on_press=self.login)
        layout.add_widget(login_button)
        return layout
    def login(self, instance):
        # Example login function
        username = "user"
        password = "pass"
        if self.login_manager.login(username, password):
            print("Login successful")
        else:
            print("Login failed")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    MainApp().run()
```

login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash
class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()
    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')
    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False
    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json
class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()
    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []
    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)
    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False
    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True
    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```

photo_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles photo uploads for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import os
from PIL import Image
class PhotoManager:
    def __init__(self, upload_directory="uploads"):
        self.upload_directory = upload_directory
        if not os.path.exists(self.upload_directory):
            os.makedirs(self.upload_directory)
    def upload_photo(self, photo_path):
        '''
        Uploads a photo to the designated upload directory.
        '''
        try:
            # Open the image to ensure it's valid
            with Image.open(photo_path) as img:
                img.verify()  # Verify that this is an image file
            # Copy the file to the upload directory
            file_name = os.path.basename(photo_path)
            destination_path = os.path.join(self.upload_directory, file_name)
            with open(photo_path, 'rb') as src_file:
                with open(destination_path, 'wb') as dest_file:
                    dest_file.write(src_file.read())
            return destination_path
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to upload photo: {e}")
            return None
```

ocr_manager.py
```python
'''
Integrates OCR functionality for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import pytesseract
from PIL import Image
class OCRManager:
    def process_image(self, image_path):
        # Extract text from image using OCR
        image = Image.open(image_path)
        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image)
        return text
```

cloud_storage_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages cloud storage for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import boto3
class CloudStorageManager:
    def __init__(self, bucket_name):
        self.s3 = boto3.client('s3')
        self.bucket_name = bucket_name
    def upload_file(self, file_path, key):
        self.s3.upload_file(file_path, self.bucket_name, key)
    def download_file(self, key, file_path):
        self.s3.download_file(self.bucket_name, key, file_path)
```

digital_signature_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles digital signatures for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA
class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature
    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```

```python
'''
Main application file for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from kivy.app import App
from kivy.uix.button import Button
from kivy.uix.boxlayout import BoxLayout
from login_manager import LoginManager
from logbook_manager import LogbookManager
from photo_manager import PhotoManager
from ocr_manager import OCRManager
from cloud_storage_manager import CloudStorageManager
from digital_signature_manager import DigitalSignatureManager
class MainApp(App):
    def build(self):
        self.login_manager = LoginManager()
        self.logbook_manager = LogbookManager()
        self.photo_manager = PhotoManager()
        self.ocr_manager = OCRManager()
        self.cloud_storage_manager = CloudStorageManager(bucket_name="your_bucket_name")
        self.digital_signature_manager = DigitalSignatureManager(private_key_path="path/to/private_key.pem", public_key_path="path/to/public_key.pem")
        layout = BoxLayout(orientation='vertical')
        login_button = Button(text="Login")
        login_button.bind(on_press=self.login)
        layout.add_widget(login_button)
        return layout
    def login(self, instance):
        # Example login function
        username = "user"
        password = "pass"
        if self.login_manager.login(username, password):
            print("Login successful")
        else:
            print("Login failed")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    MainApp().run()
```

login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash
class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()
    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')
    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False
    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json
class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()
    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []
    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)
    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False
    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True
    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```

photo_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles photo uploads for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import os
from PIL import Image
class PhotoManager:
    def __init__(self, upload_directory="uploads"):
        self.upload_directory = upload_directory
        if not os.path.exists(self.upload_directory):
            os.makedirs(self.upload_directory)
    def upload_photo(self, photo_path):
        '''
        Uploads a photo to the designated upload directory.
        '''
        try:
            # Open the image to ensure it's valid
            with Image.open(photo_path) as img:
                img.verify()  # Verify that this is an image file
            # Copy the file to the upload directory
            file_name = os.path.basename(photo_path)
            destination_path = os.path.join(self.upload_directory, file_name)
            with open(photo_path, 'rb') as src_file:
                with open(destination_path, 'wb') as dest_file:
                    dest_file.write(src_file.read())
            return destination_path
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to upload photo: {e}")
            return None
```

ocr_manager.py
```python
'''
Integrates OCR functionality for the Digital Diver's Logbook.

import pytesseract
from PIL import Image
class OCRManager:
    def process_image(self, image_path):
        # Extract text from image using OCR
        image = Image.open(image_path)
        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image)
        return text
```

cloud_storage_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages cloud storage for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import boto3
class CloudStorageManager:
    def __init__(self, bucket_name):
        self.s3 = boto3.client('s3')
        self.bucket_name = bucket_name
    def upload_file(self, file_path, key):
        self.s3.upload_file(file_path, self.bucket_name, key)
    def download_file(self, key, file_path):
        self.s3.download_file(self.bucket_name, key, file_path)
```

digital_signature_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles digital signatures for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA
class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature
    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main application file for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from kivy.app import App
from kivy.uix.button import Button
from kivy.uix.boxlayout import BoxLayout
from login_manager import LoginManager
from logbook_manager import LogbookManager
from photo_manager import PhotoManager
from ocr_manager import OCRManager
from cloud_storage_manager import CloudStorageManager
from digital_signature_manager import DigitalSignatureManager
class MainApp(App):
    def build(self):
        self.login_manager = LoginManager()
        self.logbook_manager = LogbookManager()
        self.photo_manager = PhotoManager()
        self.ocr_manager = OCRManager()
        self.cloud_storage_manager = CloudStorageManager(bucket_name="your_bucket_name")
        self.digital_signature_manager = DigitalSignatureManager(private_key_path="path/to/private_key.pem", public_key_path="path/to/public_key.pem")
        layout = BoxLayout(orientation='vertical')
        login_button = Button(text="Login")
        login_button.bind(on_press=self.login)
        layout.add_widget(login_button)
        return layout
    def login(self, instance):
        # Example login function
        username = "user"
        password = "pass"
        if self.login_manager.login(username, password):
            print("Login successful")
        else:
            print("Login failed")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    MainApp().run()
```

login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash
class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()
    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')
    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False
    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json
class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()
    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []
    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)
    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False
    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True
    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```

photo_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles photo uploads for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import os
from PIL import Image
class PhotoManager:
    def __init__(self, upload_directory="uploads"):
        self.upload_directory = upload_directory
        if not os.path.exists(self.upload_directory):
            os.makedirs(self.upload_directory)
    def upload_photo(self, photo_path):
        '''
        Uploads a photo to the designated upload directory.
        '''
        try:
            # Open the image to ensure it's valid
            with Image.open(photo_path) as img:
                img.verify()  # Verify that this is an image file
            # Copy the file to the upload directory
            file_name = os.path.basename(photo_path)
            destination_path = os.path.join(self.upload_directory, file_name)
            with open(photo_path, 'rb') as src_file:
                with open(destination_path, 'wb') as dest_file:
                    dest_file.write(src_file.read())
            return destination_path
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to upload photo: {e}")
            return None
```

ocr_manager.py
```python
'''
Integrates OCR functionality for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import pytesseract
from PIL import Image
class OCRManager:
    def process_image(self, image_path):
        # Extract text from image using OCR
        image = Image.open(image_path)
        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image)
        return text
```

cloud_storage_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages cloud storage for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import boto3
class CloudStorageManager:
    def __init__(self, bucket_name):
        self.s3 = boto3.client('s3')
        self.bucket_name = bucket_name
    def upload_file(self, file_path, key):
        self.s3.upload_file(file_path, self.bucket_name, key)
    def download_file(self, key, file_path):
        self.s3.download_file(self.bucket_name, key, file_path)
```

digital_signature_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles digital signatures for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA
class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature
    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```

```python
'''
Main application file for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from kivy.app import App
from kivy.uix.button import Button
from kivy.uix.boxlayout import BoxLayout
from login_manager import LoginManager
from logbook_manager import LogbookManager
from photo_manager import PhotoManager
from ocr_manager import OCRManager
from cloud_storage_manager import CloudStorageManager
from digital_signature_manager import DigitalSignatureManager
class MainApp(App):
    def build(self):
        self.login_manager = LoginManager()
        self.logbook_manager = LogbookManager()
        self.photo_manager = PhotoManager()
        self.ocr_manager = OCRManager()
        self.cloud_storage_manager = CloudStorageManager(bucket_name="your_bucket_name")
        self.digital_signature_manager = DigitalSignatureManager(private_key_path="path/to/private_key.pem", public_key_path="path/to/public_key.pem")
        layout = BoxLayout(orientation='vertical')
        login_button = Button(text="Login")
        login_button.bind(on_press=self.login)
        layout.add_widget(login_button)
        return layout
    def login(self, instance):
        # Example login function
        username = "user"
        password = "pass"
        if self.login_manager.login(username, password):
            print("Login successful")
        else:
            print("Login failed")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    MainApp().run()
```

login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash
class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()
    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')
    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False
    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json
class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()
    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []
    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)
    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False
    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True
    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```

photo_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles photo uploads for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import os
from PIL import Image
class PhotoManager:
    def __init__(self, upload_directory="uploads"):
        self.upload_directory = upload_directory
        if not os.path.exists(self.upload_directory):
            os.makedirs(self.upload_directory)
    def upload_photo(self, photo_path):
        '''
        Uploads a photo to the designated upload directory.
        '''
        try:
            # Open the image to ensure it's valid
            with Image.open(photo_path) as img:
                img.verify()  # Verify that this is an image file
            # Copy the file to the upload directory
            file_name = os.path.basename(photo_path)
            destination_path = os.path.join(self.upload_directory, file_name)
            with open(photo_path, 'rb') as src_file:
                with open(destination_path, 'wb') as dest_file:
                    dest_file.write(src_file.read())
            return destination_path
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to upload photo: {e}")
            return None
```

ocr_manager.py
```python
'''
Integrates OCR functionality for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import pytesseract
from PIL import Image
class OCRManager:
    def process_image(self, image_path):
        # Extract text from image using OCR
        image = Image.open(image_path)
        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image)
        return text
```

cloud_storage_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages cloud storage for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import boto3
class CloudStorageManager:
    def __init__(self, bucket_name):
        self.s3 = boto3.client('s3')
        self.bucket_name = bucket_name
    def upload_file(self, file_path, key):
        self.s3.upload_file(file_path, self.bucket_name, key)
    def download_file(self, key, file_path):
        self.s3.download_file(self.bucket_name, key, file_path)
```

digital_signature_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles digital signatures for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA
class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature
    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```

```python
'''
Main application file for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from kivy.app import App
from kivy.uix.button import Button
from kivy.uix.boxlayout import BoxLayout
from login_manager import LoginManager
from logbook_manager import LogbookManager
from photo_manager import PhotoManager
from ocr_manager import OCRManager
from cloud_storage_manager import CloudStorageManager
from digital_signature_manager import DigitalSignatureManager
class MainApp(App):
    def build(self):
        self.login_manager = LoginManager()
        self.logbook_manager = LogbookManager()
        self.photo_manager = PhotoManager()
        self.ocr_manager = OCRManager()
        self.cloud_storage_manager = CloudStorageManager(bucket_name="your_bucket_name")
        self.digital_signature_manager = DigitalSignatureManager(private_key_path="path/to/private_key.pem", public_key_path="path/to/public_key.pem")
        layout = BoxLayout(orientation='vertical')
        login_button = Button(text="Login")
        login_button.bind(on_press=self.login)
        layout.add_widget(login_button)
        return layout
    def login(self, instance):
        # Example login function
        username = "user"
        password = "pass"
        if self.login_manager.login(username, password):
            print("Login successful")
        else:
            print("Login failed")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    MainApp().run()
```

login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash
class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()
    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')
    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False
    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```
logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json
class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()
    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []
    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)
    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False
    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True
    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```
photo_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles photo uploads for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import os
from PIL import Image
class PhotoManager:
    def __init__(self, upload_directory="uploads"):
        self.upload_directory = upload_directory
        if not os.path.exists(self.upload_directory):
            os.makedirs(self.upload_directory)
    def upload_photo(self, photo_path):
        '''
        Uploads a photo to the designated upload directory.
        '''
        try:
            # Open the image to ensure it's valid
            with Image.open(photo_path) as img:
                img.verify()  # Verify that this is an image file
            # Copy the file to the upload directory
            file_name = os.path.basename(photo_path)
            destination_path = os.path.join(self.upload_directory, file_name)
            with open(photo_path, 'rb') as src_file:
                with open(destination_path, 'wb') as dest_file:
                    dest_file.write(src_file.read())
            return destination_path
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to upload photo: {e}")
            return None
```
ocr_manager.py
```python
'''
Integrates OCR functionality for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import pytesseract
from PIL import Image
class OCRManager:
    def process_image(self, image_path):
        # Extract text from image using OCR
        image = Image.open(image_path)
        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image)
        return text
```
cloud_storage_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages cloud storage for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import boto3
class CloudStorageManager:
    def __init__(self, bucket_name):
        self.s3 = boto3.client('s3')
        self.bucket_name = bucket_name
    def upload_file(self, file_path, key):
        self.s3.upload_file(file_path, self.bucket_name, key)
    def download_file(self, key, file_path):
        self.s3.download_file(self.bucket_name, key, file_path)
```
digital_signature_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles digital signatures for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA
class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature
    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```

```python
'''
Main application file for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from kivy.app import App
from kivy.uix.button import Button
from kivy.uix.boxlayout import BoxLayout
from login_manager import LoginManager
from logbook_manager import LogbookManager
from photo_manager import PhotoManager
from ocr_manager import OCRManager
from cloud_storage_manager import CloudStorageManager
from digital_signature_manager import DigitalSignatureManager
class MainApp(App):
    def build(self):
        self.login_manager = LoginManager()
        self.logbook_manager = LogbookManager()
        self.photo_manager = PhotoManager()
        self.ocr_manager = OCRManager()
        self.cloud_storage_manager = CloudStorageManager(bucket_name="your_bucket_name")
        self.digital_signature_manager = DigitalSignatureManager(private_key_path="path/to/private_key.pem", public_key_path="path/to/public_key.pem")
        layout = BoxLayout(orientation='vertical')
        login_button = Button(text="Login")
        login_button.bind(on_press=self.login)
        layout.add_widget(login_button)
        return layout
    def login(self, instance):
        # Example login function
        username = "user"
        password = "pass"
        if self.login_manager.login(username, password):
            print("Login successful")
        else:
            print("Login failed")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    MainApp().run()
```

login_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles user authentication for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import sqlite3
from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash
class LoginManager:
    def __init__(self, db_path="users.db"):
        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)
        self.create_users_table()
    def create_users_table(self):
        with self.conn:
            self.conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                    username TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    password_hash TEXT NOT NULL
                )
            ''')
    def login(self, username, password):
        cursor = self.conn.execute('SELECT password_hash FROM users WHERE username = ?', (username,))
        row = cursor.fetchone()
        if row and check_password_hash(row[0], password):
            return True
        return False
    def register(self, username, password):
        password_hash = generate_password_hash(password)
        try:
            with self.conn:
                self.conn.execute('INSERT INTO users (username, password_hash) VALUES (?, ?)', (username, password_hash))
            return True
        except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
            return False
```

logbook_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages logbook entries for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import json
class LogbookManager:
    def __init__(self, storage_file="logbook_entries.json"):
        self.entries = []
        self.storage_file = storage_file
        self.load_entries()
    def load_entries(self):
        # Load entries from a JSON file
        try:
            with open(self.storage_file, 'r') as file:
                self.entries = json.load(file)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.entries = []
    def save_entries(self):
        # Save entries to a JSON file
        with open(self.storage_file, 'w') as file:
            json.dump(self.entries, file, indent=4)
    def add_entry(self, entry_data):
        if self.validate_entry(entry_data):
            self.entries.append(entry_data)
            self.save_entries()
            return True
        return False
    def validate_entry(self, entry_data):
        # Validate entry data (e.g., check required fields)
        required_fields = ['date', 'location', 'depth', 'duration']
        for field in required_fields:
            if field not in entry_data:
                return False
        return True
    def export_entries(self, format='json'):
        # Export entries in the specified format
        if format == 'json':
            return json.dumps(self.entries, indent=4)
        elif format == 'csv':
            import csv
            import io
            output = io.StringIO()
            writer = csv.DictWriter(output, fieldnames=self.entries[0].keys())
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(self.entries)
            return output.getvalue()
        else:
            raise ValueError("Unsupported format")
```

photo_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles photo uploads for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import os
from PIL import Image
class PhotoManager:
    def __init__(self, upload_directory="uploads"):
        self.upload_directory = upload_directory
        if not os.path.exists(self.upload_directory):
            os.makedirs(self.upload_directory)
    def upload_photo(self, photo_path):
        '''
        Uploads a photo to the designated upload directory.
        '''
        try:
            # Open the image to ensure it's valid
            with Image.open(photo_path) as img:
                img.verify()  # Verify that this is an image file
            # Copy the file to the upload directory
            file_name = os.path.basename(photo_path)
            destination_path = os.path.join(self.upload_directory, file_name)
            with open(photo_path, 'rb') as src_file:
                with open(destination_path, 'wb') as dest_file:
                    dest_file.write(src_file.read())
            return destination_path
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Failed to upload photo: {e}")
            return None
```

ocr_manager.py
```python
'''
Integrates OCR functionality for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import pytesseract
from PIL import Image
class OCRManager:
    def process_image(self, image_path):
        # Extract text from image using OCR
        image = Image.open(image_path)
        text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image)
        return text
```

cloud_storage_manager.py
```python
'''
Manages cloud storage for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
import boto3
class CloudStorageManager:
    def __init__(self, bucket_name):
        self.s3 = boto3.client('s3')
        self.bucket_name = bucket_name
    def upload_file(self, file_path, key):
        self.s3.upload_file(file_path, self.bucket_name, key)
    def download_file(self, key, file_path):
        self.s3.download_file(self.bucket_name, key, file_path)
```

digital_signature_manager.py
```python
'''
Handles digital signatures for the Digital Diver's Logbook.
'''
from Crypto.Signature import pkcs1_15
from Crypto.Hash import SHA256
from Crypto.PublicKey import RSA
class DigitalSignatureManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path, public_key_path):
        with open(private_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.private_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
        with open(public_key_path, 'r') as file:
            self.public_key = RSA.import_key(file.read())
    def sign_data(self, data):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        signature = pkcs1_15.new(self.private_key).sign(h)
        return signature
    def verify_signature(self, data, signature):
        h = SHA256.new(data.encode('utf-8'))
        try:
            pkcs1_15.new(self.public_key).verify(h, signature)
            return True
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return False
```
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)
```

# Digital Diver's Logbook User Manual

Welcome to the Digital Diver's Logbook, a comprehensive application designed to digitize and enhance your diving experience. This manual will guide you through the installation, main features, and usage of the application.

## Table of Contents

1. [Introduction](#introduction)
2. [Installation](#installation)
3. [Main Features](#main-features)
4. [Usage](#usage)
5. [Troubleshooting](#troubleshooting)

## Introduction

The Digital Diver's Logbook is a cross-platform application available on Android, iOS, Windows, Mac, and Linux. It allows divers to maintain a digital logbook with features such as data digitization, photo uploads, digital signing, validation, OCR integration for journal entries, cloud storage support, dynamic export options, and secure login functionality.

## Installation

### Prerequisites

Ensure you have Python installed on your system. You can download it from [python.org](https://www.python.org/downloads/).

### Quick Install

1. Clone the repository to your local machine:
   ```bash
   git clone https://github.com/your-repo/digital-divers-logbook.git
   cd digital-divers-logbook
   ```

2. Install the required dependencies using pip:
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. Set up your environment variables for cloud storage and digital signatures:
   - Replace `your_bucket_name` in `main.py` with your actual S3 bucket name.
   - Provide paths to your private and public key files in `digital_signature_manager.py`.

## Main Features

- **Secure Login**: User authentication using hashed passwords.
- **Logbook Management**: Add, validate, and export dive entries.
- **Photo Uploads**: Upload and manage dive photos.
- **OCR Integration**: Extract text from images for journal entries.
- **Cloud Storage**: Store and retrieve data from AWS S3.
- **Digital Signatures**: Sign and verify logbook entries for authenticity.

## Usage

### Starting the Application

Run the main application file:
```bash
python main.py
```

### Logging In

1. Click the "Login" button.
2. Enter your username and password.
3. If you are a new user, register by calling the `register` method in `login_manager.py`.

### Managing Logbook Entries

- **Add Entry**: Use the `add_entry` method in `logbook_manager.py` to add a new dive entry.
- **Validate Entry**: Ensure all required fields are filled before saving.
- **Export Entries**: Export your logbook in JSON or CSV format using the `export_entries` method.

### Uploading Photos

- Use the `upload_photo` method in `photo_manager.py` to upload dive photos.

### Using OCR

- Process images to extract text using the `process_image` method in `ocr_manager.py`.

### Cloud Storage

- Upload and download files using methods in `cloud_storage_manager.py`.

### Digital Signatures

- Sign data using the `sign_data` method and verify signatures with `verify_signature` in `digital_signature_manager.py`.

## Troubleshooting

- **Login Issues**: Ensure your username and password are correct. Check the database connection in `login_manager.py`.
- **Photo Upload Errors**: Verify the image file is valid and the upload directory exists.
- **OCR Failures**: Ensure `pytesseract` is correctly installed and configured.
- **Cloud Storage Problems**: Check your AWS credentials and bucket permissions.
- **Digital Signature Errors**: Verify the paths to your RSA key files are correct.

For further assistance, please contact our support team or refer to the documentation provided in the repository.

Thank you for choosing the Digital Diver's Logbook. Happy diving!

- Upload and download files using methods in `cloud_storage_manager.py`.

### Digital Signatures

- Sign data using the `sign_data` method and verify signatures with `verify_signature` in `digital_signature_manager.py`.

## Troubleshooting

- **Login Issues**: Ensure your username and password are correct. Check the database connection in `login_manager.py`.
- **Photo Upload Errors**: Verify the image file is valid and the upload directory exists.
- **OCR Failures**: Ensure `pytesseract` is correctly installed and configured.
- **Cloud Storage Problems**: Check your AWS credentials and bucket permissions.
- **Digital Signature Errors**: Verify the paths to your RSA key files are correct.

For further assistance, please contact our support team or refer to the documentation provided in the repository.
